üöÄ NEXT STEPS FOR YOUR THESIS:

1. MERGE WITH REIT PERFORMANCE DATA:
   ```python
   # Load your REIT performance data (returns, FFO, occupancy, etc.)
   performance = pd.read_csv('your_reit_performance_data.csv')

   # Merge on ticker and year
   analysis_df = pd.read_csv('data/results/mnir/genai_index_analysis_ready.csv')
   merged = performance.merge(analysis_df, on=['ticker', 'year'], how='inner')
   ```

2. RUN REGRESSION ANALYSIS:
   ```python
   import statsmodels.formula.api as smf

   # Basic regression
   model = smf.ols('returns ~ genai_productivity_index + rating + review_count',
                   data=merged).fit()
   print(model.summary())

   # Difference-in-differences
   model_did = smf.ols('''returns ~ genai_productivity_index * post_chatgpt +
                          rating + review_count''', data=merged).fit()
   print(model_did.summary())
   ```

3. PANEL REGRESSION WITH FIXED EFFECTS:
   ```python
   from linearmodels import PanelOLS

   # Set panel index
   merged_panel = merged.set_index(['ticker', 'year'])

   # Entity (firm) fixed effects
   model_fe = PanelOLS.from_formula(
       'returns ~ genai_productivity_index + rating + EntityEffects',
       data=merged_panel
   ).fit(cov_type='clustered', cluster_entity=True)
   print(model_fe)
   ```

4. HYPOTHESIS TESTS:
   H1: GenAI productivity is associated with better firm performance
   H2: The relationship strengthened after ChatGPT launch (2023+)
   H3: Effect varies by property type or firm size
